06865: function bhNum(v){const n=Number(v||0);return Number.isFinite(n)?n:0;}
06866: function bhDate(v){return String(v||'').slice(0,10);}
06867: function bhAddDays(date,days){if(!date)return '';const d=new Date(date+'T12:00:00');if(Number.isNaN(d.getTime()))return '';d.setDate(d.getDate()+Number(days||0));return d.toISOString().slice(0,10);}
06868: function bhDaysLate(date){if(!date)return 0;const a=new Date(date+'T00:00:00'),b=new Date((typeof opsToday==='function'?opsToday():today())+'T00:00:00');return Math.max(0,Math.floor((b-a)/86400000));}
06869: function bhKind(d){return typeof opsSalesKind==='function'?opsSalesKind(d):(/خرسان/.test(String(d?.product||''))?'concrete':/بل[وؤ]ك/.test(String(d?.product||''))?'block':'');}
06870: function bhKindLabel(kind){return kind==='concrete'?'خرسانة':kind==='block'?'بلوك':'أخرى';}
06871: function bhSafeOps(){return typeof OPS!=='undefined'&&OPS?OPS:{deliveries:[],collections:[],maintenance:[],fuel:[],trips:[],items:[],custodies:[]};}
06872: function bhPaymentDays(client){return Math.max(0,Number(client?.days??D.cfg.days??3));}

06874: /* Invoice-to-collection reconciliation. Immediate cash/transfer is attached to the sale;
06875:    later collection receipts are allocated FIFO to the oldest outstanding invoices. */
06876: function bhClientLedger(clientId,requestedKind){
06877:   const S=bhSafeOps(),client=(D.cli||[]).find(c=>c.id===clientId)||{};
06878:   const invoices=(S.deliveries||[]).filter(d=>d.clientId===clientId&&d.status!=='returned').map(d=>({id:d.id,no:d.clientOrder||d.no||'',date:bhDate(d.date),kind:bhKind(d),product:d.product||'',quantity:bhNum(d.quantity),unit:d.unit||'',amount:bhNum(d.amount),immediatePaid:0,allocatedCollection:0,remaining:bhNum(d.amount),dueDate:bhAddDays(bhDate(d.date),bhPaymentDays(client)),source:d})).sort((a,b)=>a.date.localeCompare(b.date)||String(a.no).localeCompare(String(b.no)));
06879:   const byId=new Map(invoices.map(x=>[x.id,x])),collections=(S.collections||[]).filter(c=>c.clientId===clientId).slice().sort((a,b)=>bhDate(a.date).localeCompare(bhDate(b.date))||String(a.no||'').localeCompare(String(b.no||'')));
06880:   let unapplied=0;
06881:   const allocateTo=(inv,left)=>{if(!inv||left<=0||inv.remaining<=0)return left;const x=Math.min(left,inv.remaining);inv.allocatedCollection+=x;inv.remaining-=x;return left-x;};
06882:   collections.forEach(c=>{
06883:     let left=Math.max(0,bhNum(c.amount));
06884:     if(c.invoiceId)left=allocateTo(byId.get(c.invoiceId),left);
06885:     if(left>0&&c.allocationMode!=='invoice_only'){
06886:       const payDate=bhDate(c.date);
06887:       for(const inv of invoices){if(left<=0)break;if(!payDate||inv.date<=payDate)left=allocateTo(inv,left);}
06888:       /* Any excess is a valid advance payment. Re-evaluating the ledger after future
06889:          invoices are imported automatically consumes that credit FIFO. */
06890:       for(const inv of invoices){if(left<=0)break;left=allocateTo(inv,left);}
06891:     }
06892:     if(left>0)unapplied+=left;
06893:   });
06894:   const selected=invoices.filter(x=>!requestedKind||x.kind===requestedKind),aggregate=selected.reduce((o,x)=>{o.quantity+=x.quantity;o.sales+=x.amount;o.collections+=x.allocatedCollection;o.paid+=x.allocatedCollection;o.grossRemaining+=x.remaining;if(x.remaining>0&&x.dueDate&&x.dueDate<(typeof opsToday==='function'?opsToday():today()))o.overdue+=x.remaining;return o;},{quantity:0,sales:0,immediate:0,collections:0,paid:0,grossRemaining:0,overdue:0});
06895:   const totalPayments=collections.reduce((s,c)=>s+Math.max(0,bhNum(c.amount)),0),credit=requestedKind?0:unapplied,netBalance=aggregate.grossRemaining-credit,debitBalance=Math.max(0,netBalance),creditBalance=Math.max(0,-netBalance),openSelected=selected.filter(x=>x.remaining>0).sort((a,b)=>a.dueDate.localeCompare(b.dueDate));
06896:   return {client,invoices,selected,...aggregate,paid:requestedKind?aggregate.paid:totalPayments,remaining:debitBalance,debitBalance,creditBalance,netBalance,unapplied:credit,nextDueDate:openSelected[0]?.dueDate||'',maxDaysLate:openSelected.reduce((m,x)=>Math.max(m,bhDaysLate(x.dueDate)),0)};
06897: }

06902: function bhClientQtyText(c){const a=bhClientAggregate(c,'concrete'),b=bhClientAggregate(c,'block'),parts=[];if(a.quantity)parts.push(`${opsNum(a.quantity)} م³ خرسانة`);if(b.quantity)parts.push(`${opsNum(b.quantity)} بلوك`);return parts.join(' · ')||'لا توجد حركة';}
06903: function bhAllReceivables(){return (D.cli||[]).reduce((s,c)=>s+bhClientAggregate(c).remaining,0);}
06904: function bhAllOverdue(){return (D.cli||[]).reduce((s,c)=>s+bhClientAggregate(c).overdue,0);}

04733: /* --- QR (qrcode-generator, MIT) --- */
04734: function qrSVG(text, px){
04735:   try{
04736:     const q = qrcode(0, 'M');
04737:     q.addData(text, 'Byte');
04738:     q.make();
04739:     const n = q.getModuleCount();
04740:     const pad = 2, tot = n + pad*2, s = px/tot;
04741:     let r = `<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 ${px} ${px}" width="${px}" height="${px}" shape-rendering="crispEdges"><rect width="${px}" height="${px}" fill="#fff"/>`;
04742:     for(let y=0;y<n;y++) for(let x=0;x<n;x++) if(q.isDark(y,x))
04743:       r += `<rect x="${((x+pad)*s).toFixed(2)}" y="${((y+pad)*s).toFixed(2)}" width="${(s+0.35).toFixed(2)}" height="${(s+0.35).toFixed(2)}" fill="#0B2233"/>`;
04744:     return r+'</svg>';
04745:   }catch(e){ console.warn('qr',e); return ''; }
04746: }

04748: /* --- helpers --- */
04749: const DOT = '<span class="v dot">&nbsp;</span>';
04750: function fv(k, v, cls, extra){
04751:   const val = (v===0||v) && String(v).trim()!=='' ? `<div class="v ${cls||''}">${esc(v)}</div>` : DOT;
04752:   return `<div class="f ${extra||''}"><div class="k">${k}</div>${val}</div>`;
04753: }
04754: function fvRaw(k, html, extra){
04755:   return `<div class="f ${extra||''}"><div class="k">${k}</div>${html}</div>`;
04756: }

04733: /* --- QR (qrcode-generator, MIT) --- */
04734: function qrSVG(text, px){
04735:   try{
04736:     const q = qrcode(0, 'M');
04737:     q.addData(text, 'Byte');
04738:     q.make();
04739:     const n = q.getModuleCount();
04740:     const pad = 2, tot = n + pad*2, s = px/tot;
04741:     let r = `<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 ${px} ${px}" width="${px}" height="${px}" shape-rendering="crispEdges"><rect width="${px}" height="${px}" fill="#fff"/>`;
04742:     for(let y=0;y<n;y++) for(let x=0;x<n;x++) if(q.isDark(y,x))
04743:       r += `<rect x="${((x+pad)*s).toFixed(2)}" y="${((y+pad)*s).toFixed(2)}" width="${(s+0.35).toFixed(2)}" height="${(s+0.35).toFixed(2)}" fill="#0B2233"/>`;
04744:     return r+'</svg>';
04745:   }catch(e){ console.warn('qr',e); return ''; }
04746: }

04748: /* --- helpers --- */
04749: const DOT = '<span class="v dot">&nbsp;</span>';
04750: function fv(k, v, cls, extra){
04751:   const val = (v===0||v) && String(v).trim()!=='' ? `<div class="v ${cls||''}">${esc(v)}</div>` : DOT;
04752:   return `<div class="f ${extra||''}"><div class="k">${k}</div>${val}</div>`;
04753: }
04754: function fvRaw(k, html, extra){
04755:   return `<div class="f ${extra||''}"><div class="k">${k}</div>${html}</div>`;
04756: }

07143: <script id="binhamid-control-v4-script">
07144: (function(){
07145: 'use strict';
07146: const BH4_VERSION='2026.07.14-control-v4-fleet-reconciliation-customer-credit';
07147: const BH4_VEHICLE_STATUSES=[
07148:   ['', 'غير محدد'],['in_service','في الخدمة'],['parked','مركون / احتياطي'],['stopped','متوقف'],['maintenance','في الصيانة'],['out_of_service','خارج الخدمة'],['sold','مباع / مستبعد']
07149: ];
07150: const BH4_DIESEL_EXPECT=[['auto','حسب الحالة التشغيلية'],['yes','متوقع ظهوره في تقرير الديزل'],['no','لا يُتوقع ظهوره في تقرير الديزل']];
07151: function bh4N(v){const n=Number(v||0);return Number.isFinite(n)?n:0;}
07152: function bh4StatusLabel(v){return (BH4_VEHICLE_STATUSES.find(x=>x[0]===String(v?.operationalStatus||''))||BH4_VEHICLE_STATUSES[0])[1];}
07153: function bh4StatusClass(v){return ({in_service:'active',parked:'parked',maintenance:'maintenance',stopped:'stopped',out_of_service:'out',sold:'out'})[v?.operationalStatus]||'';}
07154: function bh4DieselExpected(v){const m=String(v?.dieselExpected||'auto');if(m==='yes')return true;if(m==='no')return false;if(v?.operationalStatus==='in_service')return true;if(['parked','stopped','maintenance','out_of_service','sold'].includes(v?.operationalStatus))return false;return null;}
07155: function bh4StatusChip(v){return `<span class="bh4-status ${bh4StatusClass(v)}">${opsEsc(bh4StatusLabel(v))}</span>`;}
07156: function bh4NormName(v){return String(v||'').normalize('NFKD').replace(/[\u064B-\u065F\u0670]/g,'').replace(/[أإآ]/g,'ا').replace(/ى/g,'ي').replace(/ة/g,'ه').replace(/[^\p{L}\p{N}]+/gu,'').toLowerCase();}
07157: function bh4DateOverlap(a1,a2,b1,b2){return (!a2||!b1||a2>=b1)&&(!b2||!a1||b2>=a1);}
07158: function bh4CustomerBalanceText(l){if(l.creditBalance>0)return `رصيد دائن ${opsMoney(l.creditBalance)} ر.س`;if(l.remaining>0)return `رصيد مدين ${opsMoney(l.remaining)} ر.س`;return 'الرصيد مسدد';}
07159: function bh4AllCredits(){return (D.cli||[]).reduce((s,c)=>s+bh4N(window.bhClientLedger(c.id).creditBalance),0);}
07160: function bh4AllDebits(){return (D.cli||[]).reduce((s,c)=>s+bh4N(window.bhClientLedger(c.id).remaining),0);}
07161: window.bh4AllCredits=bh4AllCredits;

07163: function bh4Reconciliation(from,to,vehicleId){
07164:   const rows=opsDieselRows(from,to,vehicleId||''),byVehicle=new Map();
07165:   rows.forEach(f=>{if(!f.vehicleId)return;if(!byVehicle.has(f.vehicleId))byVehicle.set(f.vehicleId,[]);byVehicle.get(f.vehicleId).push(f);});
07166:   const assets=(D.veh||[]).filter(v=>!vehicleId||v.id===vehicleId).map(v=>{
07167:     const fuel=byVehicle.get(v.id)||[],drivers=[...new Set(fuel.map(opsFuelDisplayDriver).filter(x=>x&&x!=='—'))],assigned=opsEmp(v.drv)?.name||'',assignedNorm=bh4NormName(assigned),driverMatched=!assigned||!drivers.length?null:drivers.some(x=>bh4NormName(x)===assignedNorm),openMaint=(OPS.maintenance||[]).find(m=>m.entityKind==='vehicle'&&m.entityId===v.id&&['pending_approval','approved','open','completed'].includes(m.status)),expected=bh4DieselExpected(v);
07168:     let effectiveStatus=bh4StatusLabel(v);if(!v.operationalStatus&&openMaint)effectiveStatus='في الصيانة';
07169:     const appeared=fuel.length>0,needsClass=!appeared&&expected===null,missingExpected=!appeared&&expected===true,conflict=appeared&&['parked','stopped','maintenance','out_of_service','sold'].includes(v.operationalStatus||'');
07170:     let review='مطابق';if(conflict)review='ظهر ديزل رغم أن الحالة غير تشغيلية';else if(missingExpected)review='متوقع في الخدمة ولم يظهر';else if(needsClass)review='حدد الحالة التشغيلية';else if(driverMatched===false)review='السائق في التقرير مختلف';else if(!appeared)review='لا توجد تعبئة في الفترة';
07171:     return {vehicle:v,fuel,appeared,fills:fuel.length,liters:fuel.reduce((s,x)=>s+bh4N(x.liters),0),amount:fuel.reduce((s,x)=>s+bh4N(x.cost),0),drivers,assigned,effectiveStatus,expected,needsClass,missingExpected,conflict,driverMatched,review};
07172:   });
07173:   const imports=(OPS.fuelImports||[]).filter(x=>bh4DateOverlap(x.from,x.to,from,to)),unmatched=[...new Set(imports.flatMap(x=>x.unmatchedPlates||[]))];
07174:   return {assets,rows,unmatched,total:assets.length,appeared:assets.filter(x=>x.appeared).length,notAppeared:assets.filter(x=>!x.appeared).length,needsClass:assets.filter(x=>x.needsClass).length,missingExpected:assets.filter(x=>x.missingExpected).length,conflicts:assets.filter(x=>x.conflict||x.driverMatched===false).length};
07175: }

07151: function bh4N(v){const n=Number(v||0);return Number.isFinite(n)?n:0;}
07152: function bh4StatusLabel(v){return (BH4_VEHICLE_STATUSES.find(x=>x[0]===String(v?.operationalStatus||''))||BH4_VEHICLE_STATUSES[0])[1];}
07153: function bh4StatusClass(v){return ({in_service:'active',parked:'parked',maintenance:'maintenance',stopped:'stopped',out_of_service:'out',sold:'out'})[v?.operationalStatus]||'';}
07154: function bh4DieselExpected(v){const m=String(v?.dieselExpected||'auto');if(m==='yes')return true;if(m==='no')return false;if(v?.operationalStatus==='in_service')return true;if(['parked','stopped','maintenance','out_of_service','sold'].includes(v?.operationalStatus))return false;return null;}
07155: function bh4StatusChip(v){return `<span class="bh4-status ${bh4StatusClass(v)}">${opsEsc(bh4StatusLabel(v))}</span>`;}
07156: function bh4NormName(v){return String(v||'').normalize('NFKD').replace(/[\u064B-\u065F\u0670]/g,'').replace(/[أإآ]/g,'ا').replace(/ى/g,'ي').replace(/ة/g,'ه').replace(/[^\p{L}\p{N}]+/gu,'').toLowerCase();}
07157: function bh4DateOverlap(a1,a2,b1,b2){return (!a2||!b1||a2>=b1)&&(!b2||!a1||b2>=a1);}
07158: function bh4CustomerBalanceText(l){if(l.creditBalance>0)return `رصيد دائن ${opsMoney(l.creditBalance)} ر.س`;if(l.remaining>0)return `رصيد مدين ${opsMoney(l.remaining)} ر.س`;return 'الرصيد مسدد';}

07167:     const fuel=byVehicle.get(v.id)||[],drivers=[...new Set(fuel.map(opsFuelDisplayDriver).filter(x=>x&&x!=='—'))],assigned=opsEmp(v.drv)?.name||'',assignedNorm=bh4NormName(assigned),driverMatched=!assigned||!drivers.length?null:drivers.some(x=>bh4NormName(x)===assignedNorm),openMaint=(OPS.maintenance||[]).find(m=>m.entityKind==='vehicle'&&m.entityId===v.id&&['pending_approval','approved','open','completed'].includes(m.status)),expected=bh4DieselExpected(v);

07171:     return {vehicle:v,fuel,appeared,fills:fuel.length,liters:fuel.reduce((s,x)=>s+bh4N(x.liters),0),amount:fuel.reduce((s,x)=>s+bh4N(x.cost),0),drivers,assigned,effectiveStatus,expected,needsClass,missingExpected,conflict,driverMatched,review};

07143: <script id="binhamid-control-v4-script">
07144: (function(){
07145: 'use strict';
07146: const BH4_VERSION='2026.07.14-control-v4-fleet-reconciliation-customer-credit';
07147: const BH4_VEHICLE_STATUSES=[
07148:   ['', 'غير محدد'],['in_service','في الخدمة'],['parked','مركون / احتياطي'],['stopped','متوقف'],['maintenance','في الصيانة'],['out_of_service','خارج الخدمة'],['sold','مباع / مستبعد']
07149: ];
07150: const BH4_DIESEL_EXPECT=[['auto','حسب الحالة التشغيلية'],['yes','متوقع ظهوره في تقرير الديزل'],['no','لا يُتوقع ظهوره في تقرير الديزل']];
07151: function bh4N(v){const n=Number(v||0);return Number.isFinite(n)?n:0;}
07152: function bh4StatusLabel(v){return (BH4_VEHICLE_STATUSES.find(x=>x[0]===String(v?.operationalStatus||''))||BH4_VEHICLE_STATUSES[0])[1];}
07153: function bh4StatusClass(v){return ({in_service:'active',parked:'parked',maintenance:'maintenance',stopped:'stopped',out_of_service:'out',sold:'out'})[v?.operationalStatus]||'';}
07154: function bh4DieselExpected(v){const m=String(v?.dieselExpected||'auto');if(m==='yes')return true;if(m==='no')return false;if(v?.operationalStatus==='in_service')return true;if(['parked','stopped','maintenance','out_of_service','sold'].includes(v?.operationalStatus))return false;return null;}
07155: function bh4StatusChip(v){return `<span class="bh4-status ${bh4StatusClass(v)}">${opsEsc(bh4StatusLabel(v))}</span>`;}
07156: function bh4NormName(v){return String(v||'').normalize('NFKD').replace(/[\u064B-\u065F\u0670]/g,'').replace(/[أإآ]/g,'ا').replace(/ى/g,'ي').replace(/ة/g,'ه').replace(/[^\p{L}\p{N}]+/gu,'').toLowerCase();}
07157: function bh4DateOverlap(a1,a2,b1,b2){return (!a2||!b1||a2>=b1)&&(!b2||!a1||b2>=a1);}
07158: function bh4CustomerBalanceText(l){if(l.creditBalance>0)return `رصيد دائن ${opsMoney(l.creditBalance)} ر.س`;if(l.remaining>0)return `رصيد مدين ${opsMoney(l.remaining)} ر.س`;return 'الرصيد مسدد';}
07159: function bh4AllCredits(){return (D.cli||[]).reduce((s,c)=>s+bh4N(window.bhClientLedger(c.id).creditBalance),0);}
07160: function bh4AllDebits(){return (D.cli||[]).reduce((s,c)=>s+bh4N(window.bhClientLedger(c.id).remaining),0);}
07161: window.bh4AllCredits=bh4AllCredits;

07163: function bh4Reconciliation(from,to,vehicleId){
07164:   const rows=opsDieselRows(from,to,vehicleId||''),byVehicle=new Map();
07165:   rows.forEach(f=>{if(!f.vehicleId)return;if(!byVehicle.has(f.vehicleId))byVehicle.set(f.vehicleId,[]);byVehicle.get(f.vehicleId).push(f);});
07166:   const assets=(D.veh||[]).filter(v=>!vehicleId||v.id===vehicleId).map(v=>{
07167:     const fuel=byVehicle.get(v.id)||[],drivers=[...new Set(fuel.map(opsFuelDisplayDriver).filter(x=>x&&x!=='—'))],assigned=opsEmp(v.drv)?.name||'',assignedNorm=bh4NormName(assigned),driverMatched=!assigned||!drivers.length?null:drivers.some(x=>bh4NormName(x)===assignedNorm),openMaint=(OPS.maintenance||[]).find(m=>m.entityKind==='vehicle'&&m.entityId===v.id&&['pending_approval','approved','open','completed'].includes(m.status)),expected=bh4DieselExpected(v);
07168:     let effectiveStatus=bh4StatusLabel(v);if(!v.operationalStatus&&openMaint)effectiveStatus='في الصيانة';
07169:     const appeared=fuel.length>0,needsClass=!appeared&&expected===null,missingExpected=!appeared&&expected===true,conflict=appeared&&['parked','stopped','maintenance','out_of_service','sold'].includes(v.operationalStatus||'');
07170:     let review='مطابق';if(conflict)review='ظهر ديزل رغم أن الحالة غير تشغيلية';else if(missingExpected)review='متوقع في الخدمة ولم يظهر';else if(needsClass)review='حدد الحالة التشغيلية';else if(driverMatched===false)review='السائق في التقرير مختلف';else if(!appeared)review='لا توجد تعبئة في الفترة';
07171:     return {vehicle:v,fuel,appeared,fills:fuel.length,liters:fuel.reduce((s,x)=>s+bh4N(x.liters),0),amount:fuel.reduce((s,x)=>s+bh4N(x.cost),0),drivers,assigned,effectiveStatus,expected,needsClass,missingExpected,conflict,driverMatched,review};
07172:   });
07173:   const imports=(OPS.fuelImports||[]).filter(x=>bh4DateOverlap(x.from,x.to,from,to)),unmatched=[...new Set(imports.flatMap(x=>x.unmatchedPlates||[]))];
07174:   return {assets,rows,unmatched,total:assets.length,appeared:assets.filter(x=>x.appeared).length,notAppeared:assets.filter(x=>!x.appeared).length,needsClass:assets.filter(x=>x.needsClass).length,missingExpected:assets.filter(x=>x.missingExpected).length,conflicts:assets.filter(x=>x.conflict||x.driverMatched===false).length};
07175: }
07176: window.bh4Reconciliation=bh4Reconciliation;

07178: function bh4ReconciliationTable(rec,interactive){
07179:   if(!rec.assets.length)return opsEmpty('لا توجد أصول مطابقة للنطاق','');
07180:   return `<div class="ops-table-wrap"><table class="ops-table"><thead><tr><th>رقم الأصل</th><th>اللوحة / التشغيل</th><th>النوع</th><th>السائق المعتمد</th><th>السائق في التقرير</th><th>الحالة التشغيلية</th><th>ظهوره في الديزل</th><th>اللترات</th><th>نتيجة المطابقة</th>${interactive?'<th></th>':''}</tr></thead><tbody>${rec.assets.map(x=>`<tr><td class="mono">${opsEsc(x.vehicle.acct||'—')}</td><td><b>${opsEsc(x.vehicle.plate||'—')}</b></td><td>${opsEsc(x.vehicle.type||'—')}</td><td>${opsEsc(x.assigned||'غير مُسند')}</td><td>${opsEsc(x.drivers.join('، ')||'—')}</td><td>${bh4StatusChip(x.vehicle)}<div class="muted">${x.expected===true?'متوقع بالديزل':x.expected===false?'غير متوقع بالديزل':'التوقع غير محدد'}</div></td><td>${x.appeared?`<span class="ops-status">ظهر — ${x.fills} تعبئة</span>`:'<span class="ops-status muted">لم يظهر</span>'}</td><td class="num">${x.liters?opsNum(x.liters):'—'}</td><td>${x.conflict||x.missingExpected||x.driverMatched===false?`<span class="ops-status warn">${opsEsc(x.review)}</span>`:x.needsClass?`<span class="ops-status info">${opsEsc(x.review)}</span>`:`<span class="ops-status">${opsEsc(x.review)}</span>`}</td>${interactive?`<td><button class="ops-btn ghost sm" onclick="bh4VehicleStatusForm('${x.vehicle.id}')">تحديد الحالة</button></td>`:''}</tr>`).join('')}</tbody></table></div>`;

07216: window.opsDieselControlData=function(rows){const c=bh4BaseDieselControl(rows),added=[];const add=(f,level,check,detail)=>added.push({fuelId:f.id,level,check,detail,date:f.date,plate:opsFuelDisplayPlate(f),receipt:f.receipt||f.no||'—'});(rows||[]).forEach(f=>{const v=opsVeh(f.vehicleId);if(!v)return;const assigned=opsEmp(v.drv)?.name||'',reported=opsFuelDisplayDriver(f);if(assigned&&reported&&reported!=='—'&&bh4NormName(assigned)!==bh4NormName(reported))add(f,'warn','اختلاف السائق',`المسند في الأصول: ${assigned} — الوارد بالتقرير: ${reported}`);if(['parked','stopped','maintenance','out_of_service','sold'].includes(v.operationalStatus||''))add(f,'warn','تعبئة لا تتفق مع حالة الأصل',`الحالة المسجلة: ${bh4StatusLabel(v)}`);});c.alerts.push(...added);const rank={danger:0,warn:1,info:2};c.alerts.sort((a,b)=>(rank[a.level]-rank[b.level])||String(a.date).localeCompare(String(b.date)));c.byFuel=new Map();c.alerts.forEach(a=>{if(!c.byFuel.has(a.fuelId))c.byFuel.set(a.fuelId,[]);c.byFuel.get(a.fuelId).push(a);});c.danger=c.alerts.filter(x=>x.level==='danger').length;c.warn=c.alerts.filter(x=>x.level==='warn').length;c.info=c.alerts.filter(x=>x.level==='info').length;return c;};

===== window.bhClientLedger / ORIGINAL 7147-7263 =====
07147: const BH4_VEHICLE_STATUSES=[
07148:   ['', 'غير محدد'],['in_service','في الخدمة'],['parked','مركون / احتياطي'],['stopped','متوقف'],['maintenance','في الصيانة'],['out_of_service','خارج الخدمة'],['sold','مباع / مستبعد']
07149: ];
07150: const BH4_DIESEL_EXPECT=[['auto','حسب الحالة التشغيلية'],['yes','متوقع ظهوره في تقرير الديزل'],['no','لا يُتوقع ظهوره في تقرير الديزل']];
07151: function bh4N(v){const n=Number(v||0);return Number.isFinite(n)?n:0;}
07152: function bh4StatusLabel(v){return (BH4_VEHICLE_STATUSES.find(x=>x[0]===String(v?.operationalStatus||''))||BH4_VEHICLE_STATUSES[0])[1];}
07153: function bh4StatusClass(v){return ({in_service:'active',parked:'parked',maintenance:'maintenance',stopped:'stopped',out_of_service:'out',sold:'out'})[v?.operationalStatus]||'';}
07154: function bh4DieselExpected(v){const m=String(v?.dieselExpected||'auto');if(m==='yes')return true;if(m==='no')return false;if(v?.operationalStatus==='in_service')return true;if(['parked','stopped','maintenance','out_of_service','sold'].includes(v?.operationalStatus))return false;return null;}
07155: function bh4StatusChip(v){return `<span class="bh4-status ${bh4StatusClass(v)}">${opsEsc(bh4StatusLabel(v))}</span>`;}
07156: function bh4NormName(v){return String(v||'').normalize('NFKD').replace(/[\u064B-\u065F\u0670]/g,'').replace(/[أإآ]/g,'ا').replace(/ى/g,'ي').replace(/ة/g,'ه').replace(/[^\p{L}\p{N}]+/gu,'').toLowerCase();}
07157: function bh4DateOverlap(a1,a2,b1,b2){return (!a2||!b1||a2>=b1)&&(!b2||!a1||b2>=a1);}
07158: function bh4CustomerBalanceText(l){if(l.creditBalance>0)return `رصيد دائن ${opsMoney(l.creditBalance)} ر.س`;if(l.remaining>0)return `رصيد مدين ${opsMoney(l.remaining)} ر.س`;return 'الرصيد مسدد';}
07159: function bh4AllCredits(){return (D.cli||[]).reduce((s,c)=>s+bh4N(window.bhClientLedger(c.id).creditBalance),0);}
07160: function bh4AllDebits(){return (D.cli||[]).reduce((s,c)=>s+bh4N(window.bhClientLedger(c.id).remaining),0);}

07163: function bh4Reconciliation(from,to,vehicleId){
07164:   const rows=opsDieselRows(from,to,vehicleId||''),byVehicle=new Map();
07165:   rows.forEach(f=>{if(!f.vehicleId)return;if(!byVehicle.has(f.vehicleId))byVehicle.set(f.vehicleId,[]);byVehicle.get(f.vehicleId).push(f);});
07166:   const assets=(D.veh||[]).filter(v=>!vehicleId||v.id===vehicleId).map(v=>{
07167:     const fuel=byVehicle.get(v.id)||[],drivers=[...new Set(fuel.map(opsFuelDisplayDriver).filter(x=>x&&x!=='—'))],assigned=opsEmp(v.drv)?.name||'',assignedNorm=bh4NormName(assigned),driverMatched=!assigned||!drivers.length?null:drivers.some(x=>bh4NormName(x)===assignedNorm),openMaint=(OPS.maintenance||[]).find(m=>m.entityKind==='vehicle'&&m.entityId===v.id&&['pending_approval','approved','open','completed'].includes(m.status)),expected=bh4DieselExpected(v);
07168:     let effectiveStatus=bh4StatusLabel(v);if(!v.operationalStatus&&openMaint)effectiveStatus='في الصيانة';
07169:     const appeared=fuel.length>0,needsClass=!appeared&&expected===null,missingExpected=!appeared&&expected===true,conflict=appeared&&['parked','stopped','maintenance','out_of_service','sold'].includes(v.operationalStatus||'');
07170:     let review='مطابق';if(conflict)review='ظهر ديزل رغم أن الحالة غير تشغيلية';else if(missingExpected)review='متوقع في الخدمة ولم يظهر';else if(needsClass)review='حدد الحالة التشغيلية';else if(driverMatched===false)review='السائق في التقرير مختلف';else if(!appeared)review='لا توجد تعبئة في الفترة';
07171:     return {vehicle:v,fuel,appeared,fills:fuel.length,liters:fuel.reduce((s,x)=>s+bh4N(x.liters),0),amount:fuel.reduce((s,x)=>s+bh4N(x.cost),0),drivers,assigned,effectiveStatus,expected,needsClass,missingExpected,conflict,driverMatched,review};
07172:   });
07173:   const imports=(OPS.fuelImports||[]).filter(x=>bh4DateOverlap(x.from,x.to,from,to)),unmatched=[...new Set(imports.flatMap(x=>x.unmatchedPlates||[]))];
07174:   return {assets,rows,unmatched,total:assets.length,appeared:assets.filter(x=>x.appeared).length,notAppeared:assets.filter(x=>!x.appeared).length,needsClass:assets.filter(x=>x.needsClass).length,missingExpected:assets.filter(x=>x.missingExpected).length,conflicts:assets.filter(x=>x.conflict||x.driverMatched===false).length};
07175: }

07216: window.opsDieselControlData=function(rows){const c=bh4BaseDieselControl(rows),added=[];const add=(f,level,check,detail)=>added.push({fuelId:f.id,level,check,detail,date:f.date,plate:opsFuelDisplayPlate(f),receipt:f.receipt||f.no||'—'});(rows||[]).forEach(f=>{const v=opsVeh(f.vehicleId);if(!v)return;const assigned=opsEmp(v.drv)?.name||'',reported=opsFuelDisplayDriver(f);if(assigned&&reported&&reported!=='—'&&bh4NormName(assigned)!==bh4NormName(reported))add(f,'warn','اختلاف السائق',`المسند في الأصول: ${assigned} — الوارد بالتقرير: ${reported}`);if(['parked','stopped','maintenance','out_of_service','sold'].includes(v.operationalStatus||''))add(f,'warn','تعبئة لا تتفق مع حالة الأصل',`الحالة المسجلة: ${bh4StatusLabel(v)}`);});c.alerts.push(...added);const rank={danger:0,warn:1,info:2};c.alerts.sort((a,b)=>(rank[a.level]-rank[b.level])||String(a.date).localeCompare(String(b.date)));c.byFuel=new Map();c.alerts.forEach(a=>{if(!c.byFuel.has(a.fuelId))c.byFuel.set(a.fuelId,[]);c.byFuel.get(a.fuelId).push(a);});c.danger=c.alerts.filter(x=>x.level==='danger').length;c.warn=c.alerts.filter(x=>x.level==='warn').length;c.info=c.alerts.filter(x=>x.level==='info').length;return c;};
